  <h1>Turn One Session into a<br><em>21-Day Guided Experience</em></h1>

  <p class="hero-sub">Stop relying on verbal instructions or unread emails. Daily Spark Manager extends your care beyond the office — keeping clients engaged, supported, and consistent.</p>

<div class="compare-section">

  <div class="section-inner">

    <p class="label">The Shift</p>

    <h2>From Session-Based<br>to Continuous Engagement</h2>

    <p class="section-desc">The traditional model leaves a 48-hour window where client momentum collapses. Daily Spark closes that gap permanently.</p>

    <div class="compare-grid">

      <div class="compare-head prob">The Traditional Problem</div>

      <div class="compare-head sol">The Daily Spark Solution</div>

      <div class="c-cell prob">Verbal homework is forgotten or misunderstood within days.</div>

      <div class="c-cell sol">Standardized 21-day guided paths delivered directly to mobile devices.</div>

      <div class="c-cell prob">Zero visibility into whether clients practice between appointments.</div>

      <div class="c-cell sol">Real-time activity logs showing exactly who engages with their Sparks.</div>

      <div class="c-cell prob">Engagement drops significantly 48 hours after a session.</div>

      <div class="c-cell sol">Automated daily reminders and structured content keep momentum high.</div>

    </div>
